 After marriage, the accused groom was again sent to jail, while the girl went to her mckay
 darasal maamla teen saal purana he
 The girl, who hails from Gennadih in Gidhaur police station area of jamui, fell in love with Vyas Pandey, a resident of Guguldih village of Laxmipur police station area
 is bich donon ne shaareerik sambandh bhi bana liye
 But when the girl's family came to know about the love affair between the two, they started pressuring the boy for marriage
 lekin ladke ne apane parivaar waalon ke dabaav menshaadi se inkaarkar diya
 At this, the girl took refuge in the court and filed a case of sexual abuse against the boy on the pretext of marriage
 court ke aadesh par police ne ladke ko giraftaar kar nyaayik hiraasat main jail bhej diya
 Accused Vyas Pandey was in jail for the last three years
 lekin teen saal jail main bitaane ke baad aakhirkaar ladke kaa dimag khulaa or usne court main arji di ki vah ladki se shaadi karne ko taiyaar he
 On the plea of the boy, the court asked the girl to do her will and the girl gave her consent to the court for marriage
 ladkaa or ladki donon kii sahmati jaanane ke baad court ne jail prashasan ko aadesh diya ki jail main hi unki shaadi karwaai jaae
 On the orders of the court, the jail administration today got married to the victim girl of the accused boy in full law in the temple situated in the jail premises
 haalanki is shaadi main ladkaa paksh ke parijanon main se koi bhi shaamil nahin hua
 It is clear from this that Kilkada Paksha is also not in favor of this marriage
 iske baavjood aaropee duulhe ne apni patni kaa puraa saath dene kaa vaada kiya he
 The girl also looked quite happy
 ladki ne shaadi ke baad kaha ki har pyaar karne waalon ko shaadi kerani chahie
 Initial investigations into the Congress Twitter account of the Congress vice-president Rahul Gandhi and the official Twitter accounts of the Congress Party revealed that the system of the hackers used by the server was in Bangalore
 sutron kii maane to havers ne jis ypi adress kaa istemaal kiya he, vah norge yaa sweden kaa paaya gaya he
 According to the Times of India, the police suspect that Rahul Gandhi's Twitter account was hacked from a device that did not have the updated anti-virus software installed or used another IP address
 police kii maane to havers ne alag-alag ypi adress se log in kiya hoga taaki unhen aasaani se trek nahin kiya ja sake
 Explaining the method of hacking, 'spear fishing'police also feared that malware was present in the system from which Twitter accounts were logged
 cybar expartsane hekking ke is tareeke ko 'spear fishing' bataaya, jisamen twitor handle banane ke liye i-mail acount kaa istemaal kiya jaataa he yaa phir fishing software ke jariye twitor acount ko hi hack kar liya jaataa he
 Cyber security Team was formed
 Let us know that the Cyber security Team has been formed under the leadership of DCP Anresh Roy to investigate the Rahul Gandhi and Congress Party Twitter accounts hack case
 is maamle main jaanch team ne twitor se bhi sambandhit jaankaree muhaiyaa karaae jane kii madad maangi he
 The hackers had made objectionable tweets, saying that the Twitter account of Congress Vice President Rahul Gandhi was hacked on Wednesday
 havers ne congress party or gandhi parivaar ko lekar kaiapattijanak twitakiye the
 a day later, the official Twitter account of the Congress Party was also hacked
 iti act kii dhara-66 ke tahat maamla darjadilli police ne guuruuvaar ko congress party or rahul gandhi ke twitor acounts hack hone kii shikaayat milane ke baad do mukademe darj kiye
 The police have registered cases under Section 66 of the IT Act
 rahul gandhi ne is maamle par chintaa jataate hue kaha ki yah desh main cybar security se judaa gambhir maamla he
 BJP leaders told the hand behind the hacking, while some Congress leaders feared the BJP leaders to be behind the hacking
 is par bijepi netaa subramanyan swami ne chutki lete hue kaha ki yah rahul gandhi se naaraaz kisi congressi kaa hi kaam he

 yogi sarkaar ke khilaaf vivaadit tippanee karne vaale nilambit ipies afasar himanshu kumaar kii patni priya singh pehali baar media ke saamne ain hai

 Importance of worshiping Lord Ganesha: - Lord Ganesha is called Mangalamurti
 - inaki upasna se saare vighn or baadhaaen dur ho jaati hai
 - The worship of God Ganesha is best for children, education and fortune
 -ganpati kii upasnase kundali ke ashubh yoga bhi nasht ho jate hai
 Benefits of worshiping Vighnaharta done by the leaves: - Each leaf has a different color and different fragrance
 - inke rang or gandh alag-alag grahon se jude hote hai
 - These leaves are offered to Shri Ganesh with different mantras
 - khaas tareeke se ganpati ko alag-alag pattey arpit karne se manavaanchit fal miltaa he
 How to offer Ganapati leaves: - On Wednesday Yachturthi, offer leaves to Shri Ganesh
 - subah nahaakar ganpati ke saamne ghi kaa deepak jalaaen
 - Then offer modak to them
 - apnimanokamanaake anusaar mantron ke saath alag-alag pattey ganpati ko arpit karen
 - Offer at least nine leaves at one time, 108 leaves can also be offered

 - achche swasthya ke liye - 'lambodaray namah' kahkar ber kaa patta arpit karen
 - To remove the obstacle of work - Offer 'bean leaf' by saying 'vakratunday Namah'
 - maan-sammaan, yash kii prapti ke liye - 'chaturhotre namah' kahkar tejpatta chadhayen
 - For the job - Offer Kaner leaf by saying 'viktay Namah'
 - vyavsaay main laabh ke liye - 'siddhivinayakaay namah' kahkar ketki kaa patta arpit karen
 - For economic benefit - Offer Aak leaf by saying 'vinayakaaya Namah'
